# Voice queue — manual review

Generated 2026-05-24. 282 posts ≥500 chars from the main Facebook stream.

**For each post, fill ONE checkbox:**
- `[voice]` — polished, finished Gustaf-language. Will go to `sources/mine/voice/`. Quote verbatim, never paraphrase.
- `[thinking]` — your view, not yet prose. Goes to `sources/mine/thinking/`.
- `[skip]` — the bulk judge will handle it (or it's noise).
- `[private]` — exclude entirely. Not stored.

Hint: length ≥1500 chars is marked 🔴 (more likely voice). 500–1499 is 🟡.

## 1. 2009-09-29 🔴 (1677 chars)

**call:** `[x] voice`  `[ ] thinking`  `[ ] skip`  `[ ] private`

```
Det är fantastiskt vilken helig ko LAS är. Efter detta inlägget fick jag inte mindre än 73 kommentarer på facebook. Alla gällde utspel om lagen om anställningsskydd. Jag vill bara klara upp detta för att alla skall förstå mitt syfte.

<oviktigt>
Ja, jag tycker att det finns vissa fel i LAS. Det är en lag som skrevs för snart 30 år sen och som inte är anpassad för dagens arbetsmarknad. Resultatet blir att lagen i vissa fall till och med skadar arbetstagares intressen och i väldigt många fall skadar företags intressen på ett sådant sätt att det går ut över arbetstagare.

Nej, jag tycker inte att lag skall skrotoas. Ett starkt arbetsskydd är viktigt och jag vill absolut inte ha samma arbetsmarknadspolitik som i USA, där man kan komma till jobbet en dag och upptäcka att dom bytt lås utan att ge dig den nya nycken.
</oviktigt>

Vad som är VIKTIGT är att det inte var detta som mitt blogginlägg handlade om. Detta var bara en mening i en längre text som handlade om att göra unga arbetslösa till offer. Vad jag ville få fram var att vi inte bara kan gå och klaga på staten varje gång vi har problem utan ibland ta tag i det själva. Vi svenskar har under de senaste generationerna blivit så överbeskyddat vaggade av våra politiker att vi tror att vi måste springa till dem varje gång vi stöter på problem.
Vad jag ville säga med min text var att LAS är förbannat oviktigt. Man kan lika gärna skylla på dataspel som gjort ungdomen passiv, på daltande föräldrar som gjort sina barn bortskämda eller företag som skeppar jobb utomlands...

...en anledning skulle kunna vara tidningar som skriver artiklar där ungdomar målas ut som hjälplösa offer.

Stora varma kramar,

Gustaf
```

Nu tjänar storbolagen pengar på spotify också...
Recap: De 4 stora musikbolagen (+ ett mindre) gick fick ägarandelar i Spotify i utbyte mot att ge företaget ett fördelaktigt licensavtal på deras musik. På så sätt fick både bolagen och artisterna mindre pengar per låt, men bolagen får igen detta i form av vinst på sin ägarandel
Lady Gagas Pokerface, den mest spelade låten under förra sommaren drog under en femmånadersperiod in hela 1150 kr. Samma år gick Spotify med 14 miljoner kr i vinst.
Undrar vem som blåser artister på mest pengar? Sony eller The Pirate Bay?
```

## 3. 2011-11-28 🟡 (1102 chars)

**call:** `[ ] voice`  `[ ] thinking`  `[x] skip`  `[ ] private`

```
Steg 1 - Biljetter!
Kort summering: Du kommer troligtvis att vilja köpa biljetter i Januari. Återkommer om detta.

Längre text:
Som många av er säkert hört så blev Burning Man för första gången slutsålt förra året. Därför har de i år hittat på en väldigt invecklat lotterisystem för att skapa någon form av (kraftigt kritiserad) rättvisa. Hursomhelst så är det hög tid att börja titta på sitt biljettinköp!
Biljetterna kommer att säljas i tre omgångar. En dyr "pre-sale" ($420, 3000 biljetter) som öppnas idag. Ett huvudlotteri (40 000) med tre olika nivåer på biljettpriser ($240, $320, $390) i januari, samt ett sent lotteri ($390, 10 000) i mars.

Mitt tips är att om ni inte bryr er om biljettkostnader så signar ni upp er direkt, men det kommer med största säkerhet inte vara något problem att få en biljett i januarirundan. Har ni tankar på att ha med er sällskap så kan man köpa 4 biljetter per person i första och sista rundan och 2 biljetter i huvudrundan.

Jag ber om ursäkt för att detta verkar så krångligt, men det är så det är :)
Se till att få er själva en biljett! Allt annat löser sig!
```

Hej!
Jag har en extra biljett över till StartupSweden, som startar i morgon. Detta är ett 48-timmars camp där man skall försöka bygga och lansera en ny webbtjänst. Vi har ett lag och en grym idé, men har fått ett avhopp och har en biljett över.
Eventet pågår mellan kl. 18 i morgon till kl. 18 på Fredag. Om du inte bor i Stockholm kan du sova på min soffa (bor rätt över gatan från eventet). Biljetten är redan betald, men i övrigt får du betala egna omkostnader.
Vi behöver någon som kan html, css, php, wordpress, analytics, cpc, och conversion-optimisering i valfritt urval (ju fler dess bättre).

Maila mig på guff@guff.se om du är intresserad. Skriv gärna med vad du är bra på :)

För det andra så ligger där ett videoklipp som sprider skräcken för att gmo-potatis skall sprida sig. Men, Amflora är bara manipulerad så att en typ av stärkelse (av dom två som normalt finns i potatis) inte produceras, för att kunna vara nyttigare i industriell produktion. ```
"Sist in, först ut"-regeln:
* Prioriterar senioritet över kompetens.
* Låser in människor i jobb de inte vill ha. Man vågar inte byta, eftersom man då hamnar sist och vet att man är den som först ryker vid nästa nedgång.
* Diskriminerar unga, som aldrig har haft en chans att bygga upp en lång anställning i en statisk arbetsmarknad.
* Dömer ut de som inte vill satsa på guldklocka utan som vill uppleva många olika karriärer och arbetsuppgifter i sina liv.
* Skadar företag som vid nedgång kan tvingas att sparka sina bästa till förmån för de som varit där längst. I just en nedgång kan detta vara ödesdigert för ett mindre företag.

Till nytta för vad? Trygghet för folk som inte gör sitt jobb?

Dags att Moderaterna skärper sig och slutar försvara en föråldrad industriell arbetarmodell.
```

```
Jaha, ja. Då blir det SVT Debatt ikväll igen. Ungdomsarbetslöshet den här gången. Jag har tre poänger:
* Med fler och fler uppgifter som kan skötas av datorer och maskiner, kan vi verkligen förvänta oss att det även i framtiden skall vara mänsklighetens syfte att ha ett "arbete"?
* Ungdomsarbetslösheten är bara en effekt av ett genomgående åldersdiskriminerande system, som finns i både lagar, avtal och kultur. Såklart vi inte kan ha ett system där senioritet prioriteras över kompetens. (skrota LAS osv.)
* Att prata om vem som "skall få" jobben blandas ofta ihop med hur vi skall skapa jobb, vem som skall göra detta och vilken typ av jobb som skall skapas.

Vad tycker ni är viktigast att man tar upp?
```

## 10. 2012-03-12 🟡 (1230 chars)

**call:** `[ ] voice`  `[ ] thinking`  `[ ] skip`  `[ ] private`  `[x] quote`

```
People are taking the piss out of you everyday. They butt into your life, take a cheap shot at you and then disappear. They leer at you from tall buildings and make you feel small. They make flippant comments from buses that imply you’re not sexy enough and that all the fun is happening somewhere else. They are on TV making your girlfriend feel inadequate. They have access to the most sophisticated technology the world has ever seen and they bully you with it. They are The Advertisers and they are laughing at you.

You, however, are forbidden to touch them. Trademarks, intellectual property rights and copyright law mean advertisers can say what they like wherever they like with total impunity.

Fuck that. Any advert in a public space that gives you no choice whether you see it or not is yours. It’s yours to take, re-arrange and re-use. You can do whatever you like with it. Asking for permission is like asking to keep a rock someone just threw at your head.

You owe the companies nothing. Less than nothing, you especially don’t owe them any courtesy. They owe you. They have re-arranged the world to put themselves in front of you. They never asked for your permission, don’t even start asking for theirs.

- Banksy
```

Om man läser utskottsförslaget så ser man dels att detta är ett EU-direktiv som måste genomföras. Man kan också se att det inte finns några reservationer till förslaget. När jag skrev summeringen så noterade jag att det låg en reservation från SD, MP och V, som jag tyckte var väldigt relevant att lägga med. Vad tycker ni om att jag gjorde så?
Tycker ni den ser okej ut i övrigt?

## 19. 2014-05-15 🔴 (1609 chars)

**call:** `[ ] voice`  `[ ] thinking`  `[ ] skip`  `[ ] private`

```
Dear co-creators,

As you all know, on May 4 we announced that The Borderland 2014 had reached maximum capacity. The number of co-creators was consciously capped to 300 for this year (100% growth) so as to develop the physical event in a sustainable way. What we didn’t account for however, was that our vendor counted child registrations towards that total which was not our intention. It follows that we now have 280 registered adult co-creators and 20 registered children. This means we will open up for the registration of 20 more adult co-creation membership and an any additional children.

 
After an exhaustive discussion the board has come to the decision that these 20 memberships are to be released for SEK 400. The only fair and transparent way we can see this working is through a standard first-come, first-served process. That means opening registration for the 20 spots at a time when most people should be able to access the website, with plenty of advance notice. Still, as we are aware that demand is higher than what the event can accommodate, these extra 20 spots won't change the fact that not everyone who want to will be able to go. We strongly encourage you to make your decision early whether to attend future events. You should not expect additional memberships to become available in this fashion again.

 
The co-creator registrations will open up on Sunday, May 25th at 20:00 CET.

Only people that are not already registered

I.e. If you are already registered as a co-creator you can’t register again.

There’s no limit to how many kids (up to 12 years) that can be registered.
```

## 21. 2014-05-30 🔴 (1672 chars)

**call:** `[ ] voice`  `[ ] thinking`  `[x] skip`  `[ ] private`

```
Looking for a camp? Join us at The Border!

First impressions last!
The first hug you get as you enter The Borderland will be a part of you for the entire week, maybe for the rest of your life. We wants to ensure that every dreamer who has found their way to the borderland of reality gets greeted with respect, love and encouragement.
The Border camp will help the new arrivals to find who they want to be at The Borderland (and help them dress accordingly). The plan is to bring a 6m container and have that as a "pimping station" and ritual space. This also functions as protection from the forces of nature and becomes a solid structural part of our chill out space, kitchen and bar.

The camp will be located just where the main road enters the quarry, close to bot the ocean and the potties (!), and a couple of hundred meters away from the main hoolabaloo. As shown on this map:
https://www.evernote.com/shard/s19/sh/3027cabb-57c3-4f74-8770-e724c1b2e15c/8daada6768561e08f550c86984b3c96d

What we plan to have in our camp:
* Pimping station (thrift, re-make, make up)
* A secret, dark, ritual space inside the container.
* A glorious chill out space!
* A nice bar.
* Kitchen, dishwashing, recycling station.
* Shade / rain protection.
* Sound!
* Electricity!
* Fire!

The camp is completely co-created. What's described above is a loose framework. Bring your own ideas, projects and stuff to fill out the space! No one is in charge, everyone has a responsibility to figure out what needs to be done and get it done. The common budget will hopefully pay for most things, but it is up to _all_ of us to help organize, shop, build, clean... do things :)

Sign up below!
```

## 22. 2014-08-18 🟡 (836 chars)

**call:** `[ ] voice`  `[ ] thinking`  `[x] skip`  `[ ] private`

```
I GOT MY TICKET BACK!!!
Full story: Yesterday afternoon I went to pick up my Burning Man ticket. After walking home for about 10 minutes I realize it is not in my pocket anymore. In despair, I spend 1,5 hours searching the streets of the Mission and find nothing. I finally give up and head home, taking the loss and starting the chase to buy a new ticket. One of the places I check is Craigslist, where I also posted the message "Dropped my ticket! Need a new one!"
Today I get an email with one line: "where did you drop it?". Not getting my hopes up just yet, I write back and describe my route.
The message back tells me: "Yep, I found your ticket on Van Ness yesterday. I'm willing to bet it was yours."
What insanity is this? I dropped my ticket on the streets of San Francisco and I GOT IT BACK!
Playa magic hits early this year!
```

"VI BARA LYDER
Roland Paulsen skriver in sig på Arbetsförmedlingen och hamnar snabbt i gräl med sin handläggare om åtgärdernas meningslöshet. När han återvänder är det för att genomföra en sociologisk studie om ”funktionell dumhet”.

```
"Let's suppose that you were able every night to dream any dream that you wanted to dream, and that you could, for example, have the power within one night to dream 75 years of dreams, or any length of time you wanted to have.
And you would, naturally as you began on this adventure of dreams, you would fulfill all your wishes. You would have every kind of pleasure you could conceive.
And after several nights, of 75 years of total pleasure each, you would say 'Well, that was pretty great. But now let's have a surprise. Let's have a dream which isn't under control. Where something is gonna happen to me that I don't know what it's gonna be.'
And then you would get more and more adventurous, and you would make further and further out gambles as to what you would dream.
And finally, you would dream where you are now."
~Alan Watts
```

## 41. 2015-11-16 🔴 (1770 chars)

```
I don't know if this picture is true.
When I look around everyone I know is talking about Beirut, not Paris. All I see are posts just like this, telling me that the "media" is talking about something else.

I guess, I believe it is true, because I choose to believe in my "world media" - the world media specifically tailored for me by Facebook. A world media talks about compassion and democratic values, that talks about not forgetting that what happened in Paris is exactly what the refugees of Syria are running away from. Instead of seeing this narrow lens of the Eiffel tower, my "world media" has another lens showing me hundreds of pictures exactly like this one.

This is what is called the "filter bubble", and it has never been as evident to me as the last few days. This is the global AI, alive and in action, controlling our lives, making us read only what it thinks we would prefer to read. It knows this is how we see the world and it does everything it can to help us confirm it.

It scares me that all I can see around me is openness and hope in the face of hatred and death. To me, it means that I'm getting fed a very narrow picture of the world. Not the one this drawing is showing, but still a very clearly defined and polished viewpoint of a complex and scary world. It also means that I live in a world separate from those whose minds i might want to change. It means whatever I say, I will always be preaching to my own choir.

The hands cropping the picture are not the hands of the "world media", because the hands are not hands of any human. Those are the hands of the AI.

These are hands that are just as diligent, just as coldly calculating for my little bubble of self-proclaimed do-gooders and world-saviors as they are for everyone else.
```

## 43. 2015-12-02 🔴 (1782 chars)

**call:** `[ ] voice`  `[x] thinking`  `[ ] skip`  `[ ] private`

```
Everyone is on about Zuckerberg giving 99% of his Facebook shares to a charitable foundation. Of course, this is an awesome thing to do, and I wish more wealthy people would do the same. However, I'm not entirely convinces of the long time virtue of this.

The world is already full of passive capital. We have pension funds, oil funds, large funds in all kinds of foundations. Sure, the dividends all go to different causes, but the question is: What is the capital doing while it's growing? And who is controlling it?

There are some in initiatives that put focus on this important part of the global power structure. For example, 350.org tries to get investment funds to divest in coal. But to me, this is just the tip of the iceberg.

This passive capital is being administered by people who have no ownership of the funds, and are exposed to no personal risk. Their job is simply to make the fund grow. The obvious measure of job performance in such a profession is how much money the employee made for the fund. That's how salaries are set and bonuses are paid. There are simply no personal incentives for the investment managers to do anything else than optimizing short term growth.

The second issue is the lack of corporate leadership that passive capital brings. A company owned by passive capital will not be asked to do anything else than optimizing dividends. They basically have a brain dead zombie in the driver's seat. I'm not talking about Zuckerberg or his daughter. I'm looking 200 years down the line.

Looking at a global force like Facebook, it is it really wise, long term, to have this be owned by a foundation?

Companies should be owned by people. People have conscience, pride, empathy and values. They should not be owned by systems of rules and papers.
```

---

## 48. 2016-01-04 🟡 (826 chars)

**call:** `[ ] voice`  `[ ] thinking`  `[x] skip`  `[ ] private`

```
Check out these AWESOME PHOTOS!

So happy to have been a part of this, and so very proud of my lovely @[710302176:2048:Malin Bobeck]. 

"Those Who Affected Me is an interactive light emitting textile art installation. Suspended in mid air, over 1,5 meters tall, and 2,5 meter diameter, the four winged structure invites the audience to gently touch the textile and reacts by sending colorful ripples up and down the intricate fabric.

The custom designed jacquard textile is using optical fibers connected to about 500 individually programmable color LEDs, connected to a microcomputer. Thin, electrically conducting copper threads are woven in to create touch sensitive areas inside the fabric. The 11 meters of fabric are mounted with steel rods around a steel cylinder."

Photos by @[572453071:2048:Yann Houlberg Andersen].

Citizens! Co-creators! Everyone! I'm calling all dreamers, engineers, artists, spiritual leaders, working class heroes and sparkle ponies! Please read this. Please, please... pretty please :)

This is the Survival Guide for The Borderland. No matter if you're new to participatory events, or if you're a seasoned festival traveller, you need to read this.

Being a co-creator of The Borderland comes with many opportunities, but it also comes with responsibilities.
We all have to help handle food and sanitation.
We all have to make sure we stay safe.
We all have to help out to keep outsiders off the event area.
We all have to Leave No Trace and bring all our own trash with us from the event (no, there will be no public garbage disposal).

For one week, we create a small city for ourselves.
This is what we all need to know for this city to survive.

Please, read it.
If you have any questions, comment below.
```

I'm home again... Or rather, I'm in the home where all my stuff is stored.
23 travel days in June brought me home in Tel Aviv and New York. 19 travel days in July brought me home at The Borderland, in Ramsjöstrand and in Svanesund.
It such a lovely thing to be able to carry my home with me, in my heart and in the people I love. So empowering to know that I have the ability to create home wherever I go.
In two weeks I'm home in San Francisco and Burning Man. When I get back from there, Malin and I are creating a new home, with lovely Mattis, Sanna, Linnéa and Louise, in our new house in Stureby.
I am so fucking privileged. I don't feel I have done anything of importance to deserve this. I just won the genetic and societal lottery, blessing me with this feeling, this delusion of having a home. What responsibility does this come with?
If there is something I wish to create in this world, it is that feeling. The feeling that we belong here. That this world cares for us.
That we are home.
```

## 66. 2016-11-06 🔴 (1512 chars)

**call:** `[ ] voice`  `[ ] thinking`  `[ ] skip`  `[ ] private`

```
When I was 16 years old, i was playing a little childish Elf, fumbling through the woods at one of my first live roleplaying games. On a mountaintop overlooking the vast forrest I found an old man, the elder of the local nomadic tribe. Being a bit lost, both in character and as my 16-year-old self, he comforted me by telling the story of my life.
He told me of how I existed through the imagination of others. How I was an inhabitant "Launi", the dream world, created only in the minds of the people, through storytelling. He said that I had gotten lost in Launi and accidentally wandered in to the land of the living.

Since then, Elge have had the opportunity to tell my story many times. He helped me reflect on power, gender, leadership, psychedelics, co-creation, politics and the importance of rituals. He had the ability to break my illusions of exceptionalism, to pull me out of my ego, and make me a part of a larger, even more magical historical context.

It was a blessing that Elge chose to join us at The Borderland 2013, at which point he was already diagnosed with cancer. I got the chance to spend time with him and introduce him to Malin, who were also going through chemotherapy at the time. It was oddly clear that he had spent a lifetime in that world, before the rest of us even started dreaming of it.

On Thursday night, Elge found his way back to Launi. He's no longer lost, wandering amongst the living, but living happily in the stories we tell.

Thank you, Elge, for your friendship.
```

## 72. 2016-11-25 🟡 (1461 chars)

**call:** `[ ] voice`  `[ ] thinking`  `[ ] skip`  `[ ] private`

```
What would you like to give?

For one week, we invite the city of Stockholm to create events and meetings that cross-pollinate the ideas and practices sprung from Burning Man with the society at large. That brings together the problems and passions of our time in a collective exploration of what could be.

For one week, dozens of events will take place all over the city, with a wide range of topics, depth and formats. All of them, by the initiative of the community (yes, that's You).

So, what are You passionate about? Is it education, urban planning or dodgeball? Circus arts, the refugee crisis or techno music? Yoga, mindfulness or startups? The Burning Man Week is a space for all of our collective dreaming and hopes for the future.

All events will be guided by the 10 Principles of Burning Man, being self-reliant, inclusive and participatory. As we invite all to initiate their own events, we wish for each event to reach out in the same manner, and strive to find a diversity of background, diversity of interests and diversity of expression. A co-created week of co-created events. Weather you´re experienced or never have created an event before, this is your chance to gift what you are most passionate about.

It starts with you. Fill out our signup form and share your dreams in this Facebook group. What would you like to create?

The Burning Man Week is an invitation to find out what you love to give, and give of that as much as you can.
```

## 73. 2016-11-28 🟡 (944 chars)

**call:** `[ ] voice`  `[ ] thinking`  `[ ] skip`  `[ ] private`

```
Hey there friends. We're a group of people that plan to do an event on migration and integration during the Burning Man Week in Stockholm, March 1-7.
The Burning Man Week is a week of independently organized events that ties together Burning Man philosophy and methodology with the big issue of our time.
Migration have been on the agenda in the Burner community for a long time, with Burners Without Borders working in the Jungle and a participatory refugee camp being built by burner in Greece (and many other projects). We would like to take the opportunity of having 200 Burning Man leaders in town to explore how self-leadership and participatory working methods can be used to empower and inspire people to take action on these issues.

Please join our facebook group if you're interested.
https://www.facebook.com/groups/1800105630247636/
Our first meetup will take place next Wednesday:
https://www.facebook.com/events/1482136901801362/
```

## 78. 2016-12-09 🟡 (710 chars)

```
Varför tycker marknadsliberaler att det är så upprörande när offentliga sektorn lägger pengar på fester och konferenser, men inte ser något problem alls i att privata företag gör det mångdubbelt?
Om nu marknadens krafter är så bra, så borde det väl rimligen betyda att anledningen till att ett företag har en stor konferens eller personalfest är att det minskar personalomsättning, ökar produktivitet och gagnar slutresultatet? Varför skulle inte den offentliga sektorn få använda sig av detta fantastiska verktyg för att kunna göra sitt jobb bättre?
Eller... påstår ni att privata företag regelbundet slösar pengar i större utsträckning än offentliga bolag? Det skulle väl ändå aldrig accepteras av marknaden?
```

## 79. 2017-01-03 🔴 (4063 chars)

**call:** `[ ] voice`  `[ ] thinking`  `[ ] skip`  `[ ] private`

```
Burner’s Prayer, by Mo Lohaus

May I burn the man at home this year, and finally become a full participant.

May I kick the culture consumption habit cold turkey, and get on with resonating funky genius and vulnerable enthusiasm on my own channel, 24-7.

May I see every public space as center camp, and roll around on the ground with strangers, lovingly, and with worshipful presence, as we contact one-in-other.

May I strut my feathers, leathers, muppet cape, and naked benevolent childish soul everywhere I go, feeling fully in character.

May I trick out my apartment like a theme camp, and invite people in off the street to lavish them with gifts of presence and affection, lovingly prepared.

Because I can. Because I am rich and overflowing, and giving is why I am here.

May I share shattering rock-bottom truths with everyone, as casually as tea; like old lovers with nothing left to prove or improve on; safely settled in the silky oscillation between me and we.

May I strip the locks off my heart and hold open house with everyone I meet; on the bus, in line for groceries, or at the gas station; granting them the hallucinated embellishments of fur, goggles, nudity, and dust, and allowing myself full excitement and wonder at who they might be.

May I look past the surface and see into everyone; recognizing pirates, alien ambassadors, super-heroes, and translucent mermaids.

May I call my camp mates or show up at their houses at all hours, as easily and shamelessly as I might wander up to their tents, and never need a reason for pressing my nose on their cheek or flopping on the couch and snuggling.

May I love fully, fluidly, everyone who pulls me deeper into living, and put away any residual shame about how my love looks.

Remembering: We are in the desert! We are dusty, unkempt, and beautiful! We are mad ones and saints and divas all! And there is no expectation of tidiness!

Remembering: There will be grit and friction. There always is. But in the cathartic blessing of our meeting and self-discovery no one notices.

Remembering most of all that my emotional nakedness is my ticket to the event; past the gate and greeters, to unity and a friendly universe; always honored and gratefully received.

May I hallucinate freely, seeing Volvos as giant bunny slippers and Hondas as mobile cupcakes.

May I notice the installations of genius and wild vision all about me, the dreams made real in my daily built world, and may I touch the wide round belly of the pregnant possible with both my hands.

May I witness those around me strutting their beauty and hope, their frailty, unfinishedness, and quirky unique poised artful equilibrium above the abyss of judgment, and may I yell out my approval and applaud.

May I witness the gifting that happens every day; the trade of glances, smiles, and kind words that are as quenching and comforting in the daily wasteland of formality and alienation as popsicles and mist baths ever were.

May I burn the man every day. May I take his idealized ass down. May I take the icon of who I am supposed to be and gently release it to flame.

May I take its habits, opinions, head noise, timidity, and ego-protective arrogance and lovingly douse them with gas.

This is my religion; humbly, devotedly, and persistently performed: THAT MAN will BURN.

May I build the temple every morning, and honor and celebrate those who have sung the song of my life; who have held my life like their own dear infant in their arms.

May I build the temple every morning, be awestruck by its beauty each day, smear it with prayers and tears, and release it in holy smoke.

May I smell it burn and know that was it: This day was my whole life, and it is over.

And if I am blessed to wake once more, may I do it all again. May I do it all again more fiercely and passionately. May I do it all again more graciously, goofily, and generously.

May I do it all again, until my life measures up to the love I feel as I walk, bike, or ride an octopus through the eternal city of dreams in which my soul feels at home.
```

## 80. 2017-01-03 🔴 (4063 chars)

**call:** `[ ] voice`  `[ ] thinking`  `[ ] skip`  `[ ] private`

```
Burner’s Prayer, by Mo Lohaus

May I burn the man at home this year, and finally become a full participant.

May I kick the culture consumption habit cold turkey, and get on with resonating funky genius and vulnerable enthusiasm on my own channel, 24-7.

May I see every public space as center camp, and roll around on the ground with strangers, lovingly, and with worshipful presence, as we contact one-in-other.

May I strut my feathers, leathers, muppet cape, and naked benevolent childish soul everywhere I go, feeling fully in character.

May I trick out my apartment like a theme camp, and invite people in off the street to lavish them with gifts of presence and affection, lovingly prepared.

Because I can. Because I am rich and overflowing, and giving is why I am here.

May I share shattering rock-bottom truths with everyone, as casually as tea; like old lovers with nothing left to prove or improve on; safely settled in the silky oscillation between me and we.

May I strip the locks off my heart and hold open house with everyone I meet; on the bus, in line for groceries, or at the gas station; granting them the hallucinated embellishments of fur, goggles, nudity, and dust, and allowing myself full excitement and wonder at who they might be.

May I look past the surface and see into everyone; recognizing pirates, alien ambassadors, super-heroes, and translucent mermaids.

May I call my camp mates or show up at their houses at all hours, as easily and shamelessly as I might wander up to their tents, and never need a reason for pressing my nose on their cheek or flopping on the couch and snuggling.

May I love fully, fluidly, everyone who pulls me deeper into living, and put away any residual shame about how my love looks.

Remembering: We are in the desert! We are dusty, unkempt, and beautiful! We are mad ones and saints and divas all! And there is no expectation of tidiness!

Remembering: There will be grit and friction. There always is. But in the cathartic blessing of our meeting and self-discovery no one notices.

Remembering most of all that my emotional nakedness is my ticket to the event; past the gate and greeters, to unity and a friendly universe; always honored and gratefully received.

May I hallucinate freely, seeing Volvos as giant bunny slippers and Hondas as mobile cupcakes.

May I notice the installations of genius and wild vision all about me, the dreams made real in my daily built world, and may I touch the wide round belly of the pregnant possible with both my hands.

May I witness those around me strutting their beauty and hope, their frailty, unfinishedness, and quirky unique poised artful equilibrium above the abyss of judgment, and may I yell out my approval and applaud.

May I witness the gifting that happens every day; the trade of glances, smiles, and kind words that are as quenching and comforting in the daily wasteland of formality and alienation as popsicles and mist baths ever were.

May I burn the man every day. May I take his idealized ass down. May I take the icon of who I am supposed to be and gently release it to flame.

May I take its habits, opinions, head noise, timidity, and ego-protective arrogance and lovingly douse them with gas.

This is my religion; humbly, devotedly, and persistently performed: THAT MAN will BURN.

May I build the temple every morning, and honor and celebrate those who have sung the song of my life; who have held my life like their own dear infant in their arms.

May I build the temple every morning, be awestruck by its beauty each day, smear it with prayers and tears, and release it in holy smoke.

May I smell it burn and know that was it: This day was my whole life, and it is over.

And if I am blessed to wake once more, may I do it all again. May I do it all again more fiercely and passionately. May I do it all again more graciously, goofily, and generously.

May I do it all again, until my life measures up to the love I feel as I walk, bike, or ride an octopus through the eternal city of dreams in which my soul feels at home.

## 81. 2017-01-21 🟡 (1043 chars)

**call:** `[ ] voice`  `[ ] thinking`  `[ ] skip`  `[ ] private`

```
Advice: Reinstating the 4 week transfer deadline.
Up until last year, we had a 4 week membership transfer deadline, after which no membership could change hands. The purpose of this was to push transfers to happen earlier, to ensure that those who got to go to The Borderland would know so well enough in advance to give them adequate time to prepare. This was changed last year, to enable last minute gifting of memberships.
I would like to restore it to the system we had up until 2015.

Please fill out this form if you have any arguments for or against the proposal.

With this post, I'm initiating what's called an "advice process", which is our new model for decision making. By seeking this advice from the community, and those with expert knowledge, I will through the process be granted the power to make the decision on the matter. To read more about the advice process, and how you can do this yourself if you would like to change something, please check out the wiki page on the subject: http://wiki.theborderland.se/Advice_Process
```

## 89. 2017-04-08 🔴 (1928 chars)

**call:** `[ ] voice`  `[ ] thinking`  `[ ] skip`  `[ ] private`

```
"This is what makes the theatre of terrorism so successful. The state has created a huge space empty of political violence. This huge space acts as a sounding board, amplifying the impact of any armed attack, however small. The less political violence in a particular state, the greater the public shock at an act of terrorism. Killing 17 people in Paris draws far more attention than killing hundreds in Nigeria or Iraq. Paradoxically, then, the very success of modern states in preventing political violence make them particularly vulnerable to terrorism. An act of terror that would have gone unnoticed in a medieval kingdom can rattle much stronger modern states to their very core.

The state has stressed so many times that it will not tolerate political violence within its borders that it has no alternative but to see any act of terrorism as intolerable. The citizens, for their part, have become used to zero political violence, so the theatre of terror incites in them visceral fears of anarchy, making them feel as if the social order is about to collapse. After centuries of bloody struggles, we have crawled out of the black hole of violence, but we feel that the black hole is still there, patiently waiting to swallow us again. A few gruesome atrocities and we imagine that we are falling back in.

In order to assuage these fears, the state is driven to respond with its own theatre of security. The most efficient answer to terrorism might be good intelligence and clandestine action against the networks of money that feed terrorism. But this is not something citizens can see on television. Once its citizens have seen the terrorist drama of the World Trade Center collapsing, the state feels compelled to stage an equally spectacular counterdrama, with even more fire and smoke. So instead of acting quietly and efficiently, it unleashes a mighty storm, which fulfils the terrorists’ most cherished dreams."
```

## 93. 2017-10-16 🟡 (986 chars)

**call:** `[ ] voice`  `[ ] thinking`  `[ ] skip`  `[ ] private`

```
"Pacta sunt servanda", "agreements must be kept", the first thing every student learns in law school. The lawyers' pledge to the eternal past. 
Yes, it is often good to keep agreements. It fosters trust and makes us more able to invest in the future together.

But agreements _MUST_ not be kept.

Sometimes it turns out that we have made agreements that suck. We were uninformed, didn't understand the world or ourselves well enough to grasp the implications of the agreement or the world change as time passed. Maybe the dictator of our country that made the agreement is now gone (and the newborn children of his people are now stuck repaying his debt). Striving to keep bad agreements is stupid. And walking over dead bodies to make it so is not fostering trust or stability.

The idea that "agreements MUST be kept", that "debt HAS to be repaid" is a delusion. It is against the fundamental nature of things - it is a destructive reach for permanence in a world that keeps changing.
```

I believe we have to. The connected world invites us to take initiative and responsibility. It invites us to be creative, passionate and empathic.
But, I don't believe that you will show up with your full passionate and empathic self, if you feel that it needs to fit a certain predefined box, that only a part of you is welcome. 

We have to create the spaces, in society and in our organizations, where we all can be vulnerably human. Every job that encourages you to be an unfeeling robot will soon be replaced by an actual robot. The only thing left to want is the true "you", stuck with the eternal question of "why?".
Technology is what separates us from the other animals. It is what made us human. Technology is the force that continuously pushes us to become MORE human.

In that spirit, I have to admit, I fucking hate making this post. I feel this is egotistic boasting, and I am afraid of being judged as being self-centered. Besides, who needs more "me, me, me" in this world?
On the other hand, I am also scared of putting in effort to try to win this award. It is so much more comfortable to not try, than to put yourself out there and lose.

## 95. 2017-11-07 🟡 (1371 chars)

**call:** `[ ] voice`  `[ ] thinking`  `[ ] skip`  `[ ] private`

```
Ja, vad fan får jag för pengarna egentligen?
Frågan är snarare: "HUR fan får jag pengarna egentligen?"

Som företagsledare eller entreprenör har jag den fantastiska förmånen att få tjäna pengar på infrastruktur som betalts av skattepengar. Jag kan anställa människor som utbildats för skattepengar, som tas hand av skattefinansierad sjukvård. De kan åka på skattefinansierade vägar till mitt företagskontor, eller varför inte ta den kollektivtrafik som betalts av skatt? När de skaffar barn kan de gå i skattefinansierat dagis och skola, så att föräldrarna kan lägga fokus på sitt arbete.
Allt detta kan jag göra i fastigheter som skyddas av ett statligt våldsmonopol, i ett samhälle där vårt gemensamma åtagande mot varandra har skapat så stark trygghet att mina medarbetare inte behöver lägga pengar och energi på att varje dag behöva försvara vad äger och dem de älskar.

Skatt är inte något jag betalar för att få tjänster till mig själv. Det är en helt enkelt en kostnad i min verksamhet, pengar som jag betalar för att få den fantastiska förmånen att tjäna pengar.

Det är helt förståeligt att någon argumenterar för sänkta skatter, eller för annorlunda skatter. Men om man tror att betala skatt är samma sak som att köpa en tjänst för "egna" pengar, då har man  lite bristande ödmjukhet i relation till hur man egentligen fick tag i de där pengarna i första taget.
```

---

## 97. 2017-11-28 🟡 (1299 chars)

**call:** `[ ] voice`  `[ ] thinking`  `[ ] skip`  `[ ] private`

```
”Nu får man ju spendera, annars brinner ju pengarna inne.” En kommentar jag hört inom offentligt finansierade verksamheter inte mindre än 3 gånger de senaste veckorna.
Vaddå ”brinner inne”? Vad snackar du om?
Du har sparat pengar för svenska skattebetalare genom att genomföra ditt arbete under din utsatta budget. Sen får du av någon anledning för dig att det är din skyldighet att sätta eld på dem?

För vad betyder det egentligen att pengar inte spenderats när året är slut? Är det inte något i grunden positivt att du sparat samhället pengar? Att din verksamhet istället kunnat kompensera för andra verksamheter där pengarna var mer behövliga: Vård, skola, flyktingmottagande och sjukvård som inte riktigt lyckats vända på slantarna och därför gått över sin budget.
Istället sitter du där och tänker ”jag kanske skall löpa lite kepsar med en logga på, så att inte pengarna brinner upp i slutet av året”.
Är du helt dum i huvudet?

Nej, det är du såklart inte. Idén att pengar _måste_ spenderas innan året är så utbredd inom både offentlig verksamhet och stora bolag att det ses som självklart. I många verksamheter betyder ett överskott till och med att du tilldelas mindre pengar nästa år eftersom du inte verkade behöva dem.

Så varför inte boka nån inspirerande föreläsare istället?

God jul.
```

## 98. 2018-01-15 🔴 (1948 chars)

**call:** `[ ] voice`  `[ ] thinking`  `[ ] skip`  `[ ] private`

```
I'm asking for your advice, regarding how to handle expenses for essential work with long term development of The Borderland.

@[618346573:2048:Mathias], @[1801802251:2048:Nicklas] and I will be traveling to Gotland on Jan 26 to meet with representatives of the municipality and Cementa (land owners), to discuss the possibility of the Borderland moving to Smöjen in 2019.
I am exploring the idea that the organisation would pay for our travel expenses. This is not the first time that individuals spend money for travel to do essential work for The Borderland, and it will most certainly happen more in the future. Previously, these kind of decision have been made by the board, and my proposal is to use our Advice Process to make the decision instead. Hence this post.

Read more about The Borderland Advice Process here: http://wiki.theborderland.se/Advice_Process

My proposal is that the non-profit org will cover expenses for the three of us to travel to Gotland. Because of the timing of the meeting, taking the boat would require us to stay over night, so the most practical solution in this case is, unfortunately, to fly to Visby and rent a car there. The cost is estimated to be around 2500 sek per person.

Please provide your advice.
* What factors should I be considering when making a decision about travel expenses?
* Who should I be asking for advice before making this decision?
* What is your advice on this specific case, and what is your reasoning behind it?

The goal of this process is to make the specific decision about our trip to Visby as well as provide guidelines for how to make these decisions in the future.

This thread is not about Smöjen or the idea of moving The Borderland to Gotland in 2019. That issue can be discussed in #futurelocation on Slack, and a decision will be made by the community in May 2018. You will get to have a say. Please let this thread stay on the topic of how to handle travel expenses.
```

## 99. 2018-01-17 🟡 (1482 chars)

**call:** `[ ] voice`  `[ ] thinking`  `[ ] skip`  `[ ] private`

```
SNS konjukturråd föreslår skatteskifte från inkomstskatt till skatt på kapital. Något för Initiativet att ta till sig?
Jag tycker personligen det är långsiktigt ohållbart med inkomstskatt som primär affärsmodell för den offentliga sektorn. Här är mina tankar:
* Framtidsperspektivet - Automation kommer göra att färre lönearbetar. Vi vill ändå fortsätta uppmuntra till arbete och därför inte beskatta det.
* Fördelningsperspektivet - Idag skapas förmögenheter genom inkomst på kapital, inte genom skillnader i lön. För att bromsa den skenande ojämlikheten i kapital måste detta beskattas.
* Regionalperspektivet - Så länge kommuner har inkomstskatt som primär inkomstkälla så är incitamentet att enbart satsa på innovation och utveckling som "skapar jobb" lokalt. Kommuner måste få mandatet att sätta regional fastighetsavgift (eller kanske förslagsvis markvärdesavgift?), kanske även andra lokala skatter för att ersätta bortfallet av inkomstskatten.
* Det filosofiska perspektivet - Jag tycker personligen inte det är något konstigt att beskatta t.ex. mark, eftersom det är en tydligt begränsad resurs som går att argumentera "tillhör alla". Dock har jag alltid tyckt det varit lite konstigt att staten anser sig äga en procent av min tid. Jag satt precis och hjälpte en kompis med att strukturera upp en föreläsning (som jag ju jobbar med) i gengäld så kommer han coacha mig (hans jobb). Av nån anledning så utgör detta utbyte av tid mellan två vänner ett skattebrott. Ehh... va?
```

```
Detta är ett av de allvarligaste framtidshoten på kartan idag. EU planerar alltså att införa en lag på att allt som postas på nätet måste filtreras genom en automatisk censursmaskin för att förhindra copyrightintrång. En sådan maskin skulle fälla hellre än fria, och precis som de liknande system som existerar idag så skulle en stor tyngd ligga på storbolagens rättigheter, före den enskildes.
Att bygga en sådan maskin skulle vara väldigt komplicerat, så marknaden kommer snabbt att utgöras av bara en handfull stora aktörer (Google, Facebook, kanske nån mer), som då kommer ha makt att censurera innehåll före detta ens postad på nätet.
I förslaget ligger också en ”länkskatt” där sajtägare skulle tvingas att betala pengar om de länkar till någon annans innehåll. Precis som ovan kommer även detta ge en stor makt till ett fåtal storbolag att kräva pengar från enskilda, och väldigt lite möjlighet för kreatörer att göra det motsatta.
I förlängningen så pratar vi om ett genomgående kontrollsystem, som skall censurera och beskatta vår yttrandefrihet. Ett sådant system _får_ inte byggas. Det är ett hot mot hela vårt samhälle.

## 111. 2018-09-08 🔴 (2992 chars)

**call:** `[ ] voice`  `[ ] thinking`  `[ ] skip`  `[ ] private`

```
På Söndag kommer jag att rösta på Initiativet.

Jag har aldrig riktigt känt det varit lätt att rösta. Genom åren har det blivit både FP, C och MP. Vart än rösten fallit så har det aldrig känns riktigt rätt, trots att de jag röstat på nästan alltid "vunnit" valet.
I år så poppade det nya partiet Initiativet upp på min radar. Det är ett processcentrerat parti som lägger sitt fokus på att reformera hur beslut fattas, istället för att lägga prestige i att vinna enskilda sakfrågor. Evidens sätts centralt, lyssnandet får gå före talandet. De gör en poäng i att ha olika perspektiv representerade inom partiet, istället för att försöka få alla i samma fålla.
Partiets ideologi bygger på "The Listening Society", en bok av filosofen Hanzi Freinacht, som innehåller en mening som har fastnat i mitt huvud det senaste året:

"It must become a top political priority to support the psychological development of all citizens".

För mig är detta ett mål som står över alla andra. Ett mål som till och med står över att rädda vårt klimat. Detta mål är nämligen en förutsättning för alla andra mål. Vi kommer inte kunna rädda klimatet, vi kommer inte kunna lösa fattigdom, utanförskap eller migrationsfrågor om vi inte först sätter som mål att främja den psykologiska utveckligen hos samtliga medborgare. Utan det kommer människor varken att rösta för de politiska förändringar eller göra de förändringar i sitt liv som krävs för att t.ex. lösa klimatkrisen.
Förändring, nya valmöjligheter och ökad komplexitet kräver att var och en blir bättre rustad att hantera vår värld. Det måste bli vårt primära fokus.

Sen så är det ju såklart det här med att "kasta bort" sin röst. Jag har en stor respekt för Centerpartiet, deras kamp i migrationsdebatten och deras mod att fortsätta sätta positiva budskap i centrum. Det är ett parti som jag själv lagt energi i och där jag ser många kompetenta människor som jag också skulle vilja ge mitt stöd.

Men, som jag ser det just nu så kommer valresultatet att sluta i ett högst oklart parlamentariskt läge, som kommer avgöras genom förhandlingar och maktkamper mellan och inom partierna. Ett par procent hit eller dit på något parti kommer inte göra en stor skillnad. När, om någonsin, skall man våga lägga sin röst på något nytt?

Jag är inte så naiv att tro att Initiativet kommer få 4%, eller ens 1% (som ju är gränsen för att få valsedlar distribuerade i nästa val). Min röst är en långsiktig förhoppning om en större förändring av det politiska samtalet. Jag tänker inte rösta på det ”minst dåliga” jag vägrar rösta ”mot SD”. Jag vill spendera mitt liv på att verkligen skapa något bra, inte fortsätta stärka bilden att allt vi kan hoppas på är att få det minst dåliga.
Jag kanske inte ändrar valresultat men jag kan i alla fall ge en helhjärtad uppmuntran till de som kämpat för det närmast omöjliga projektet att ge liv till ett helt nytt parti. Min röst står för en vädjan till alla partier att våga lyfta blicken. Den står för att vilja skapa något nytt.
```

## 114. 2018-11-20 🔴 (1739 chars)

**call:** `[ ] voice`  `[ ] thinking`  `[ ] skip`  `[ ] private`

```
Här är min väns berättelse om Försäkringskassan, ett perfekt exempel på hur vi behöver en icke behovsprövad basinkomst som trygghetsnät istället för det byråkratiska härke som är sjukförsäkring...

"Det här är storyn: 
Jag blev rejält utbränd i början 2016. Jag ramlade ihop på marken ute på gatan och minns inte hur jag kom hem. Efter det följde ett par helt vansinniga veckor, det var det sjukaste jag vart med om. Jag var sängliggande, när jag reste mig upp så snurrade allting. Jag fick krypa till toaletten. Jag har alltid vart en väldigt aktiv människa och jobbat hårt så detta tärde verkligen på mig, att knappt kunna göra någonting själv och ligga i sängen 24/7. Efter ett par månader så mådde jag bättre stundtals och fick en förfrågan av mitt gamla jobb om jag ville testa jobba lite. Jag var så himla uttråkad och trött på att ligga och stirra i taket så jag blev glad och sa ja! Min läkare hade sagt att jag närsomhelst kunde testa att jobba om jag ville. Så i maj så arbetade jag en dag 7 timmar. Jag blev helt slut, det var ingen bra idé och gick direkt tillbaka till sjukskrivning. Därefter var jag sjukskriven ungefär 1 år till. 

Ungefär 2 år efter att jag arbetat 1 dag så får jag ett brev av Försäkringskassan. De hävdar att jag eftersom jag jobbat 1 dag avbröt min sjukskrivning och att jag resten av min sjukskrivning måste vart frisk. Detta trots att min sjukskrivning blev förlängd av TVÅ olika läkare efter den dagen jag jobbade. Men näpp, nån random handläggare på Försäkringskassan som jag aldrig ens pratat med tycker tydligen att de vet bättre, 2 år i efterhand. 

Så jag blev tvungen att betala tillbaka 65 557 kronor.
Jag har en avbetalningsplan på 10 år och har för närvarande 62 484 kronor kvar att betala."
```

## 121. 2019-01-23 🟡 (1252 chars)

**call:** `[ ] voice`  `[ ] thinking`  `[ ] skip`  `[ ] private`

```
But whyyyyy Roland?
4 min in to the clip, I’m ecstatic. Hans Rosling kicked in the balls in funny way, while being respectful and intelligent.
But... If your point is to criticize misleading statistics, you have to be damn sure that you are not doing the same.
I’m not saying Paulsen is necessarily wrong here, but his points on mental health are using statistics to commit exactly the same crime he is kicking Rosling for.
First of all: If you are starving you don’t complain about depression. NO SHIT that people complain more about mental problems when they don’t have any physical ones anymore. Not mentioning this is a lie by omission.
Second: Number of diagnoses =/= actual prevalence. OF COURSE rich countries with well built out and financed health care diagnoses more mental illness.
And third: increase in anti-depressant use does not equate an increase in depression more than increased sales of Head and Shoulders equate global increases in dandruff.

Yes, mental health is a problem, and it is probably increasing, just as Paulsen suggests. But if anything, what this video proves is that the real problem in society is the constant increase in misleading infographics.

Still, watch it. It’s good. Just keep your “yes, and” close to mind.
```

Nothing really. Neutral. Slight positive because it lifts some issues such as bullying and sexual harassment. Slight disgust at capitalist opportunism disguised as idealism. Thinking I’ve seen all of the situations in the ad and do recognize that most men in most situations do indeed not stand up and call folks out. Still it all comes out a bit silly, as commercials generally do.

To the offended party: I think you’re all wrong, folks. And I think that your reaction says more about yourselves than about the commercial. I think you are exact equivalents of the non-constructive, bitter, bitchy kinds of feminists and anti-racists whose toes are always perpetually stepped upon by one wrong word, some naked skin, one commercial or another.

I’m calling you out, guys: you’re being over-sensitive. You’re taking part in a silly hysteria.”
```

## 124. 2019-02-07 🟡 (675 chars)

**call:** `[ ] voice`  `[ ] thinking`  `[ ] skip`  `[ ] private`

```
Some people argue that blockchain and other digital systems can be used to manage trust. But actual trust doesn’t have to be managed by systems. Those are only needed when trust is lacking. You are using digitally managed distrust as a proxy for trust, which is in many cases needed, but not the same thing as actual trust.
This is also why many hypothesized uses of blockchain are bullshit. Blockchain is only useful when you don’t have actual trust, like for example in organized crime. Trusting a third party will always be faster and more efficient than a global number crunching crypto machine.
You only need “digital distrust systems” when you are lacking actual trust.
```

Who's a leader anyway?
Apply for The Co-Creative Leadership Development Program!

I often talk about self-organization, both in cultural and business contexts. To me, that does not mean having fewer leaders, but rather to have more of them. To have everyone step up in their own leadership. But where do we find the skill, knowledge and mindset to be those leaders?

I’m proud to invite you to The Co-Creative Leadership Development Program, a 3 month training for leaders working with co-creative event production. The program will kick of with a retreat in Stockholm on May 3-5 and follow up with online seminars and coaching over the course of the summer. It will cover leadership theory, practical skill training and personal development exercises, and will be hosted by a group of professional facilitators with experience from both festivals and the corporate world.

We are looking for 21 leaders, who might not have a lot of experience with co-creative event production, but who are dedicated to growth and learning. The program is funded by The Borderland, so two thirds of the spots will be directed for those of you who are intending to step up in leadership at this year's Borderland event. The last third of the class will be from outside The Borderland community, to provide diversity of views and backgrounds.

Those who finish the program will be awarded an official Co-Creative Leadership Diploma to put in their CVs... Because we can do that.

Does this sound like you? Do you know someone who should apply? 

Application deadline March 17.

Sign up here: https://guff.typeform.com/to/gJIxsd

```
””(Barnen) använder inte appar för att de vill lära sig någonting eller förbereda sig för framtiden. De gör det för att det är roligt”, konstaterar hon. Gör man ett pedagogiskt geografispel försöker ungarna få många poäng, inte tillägna sig bestående kunskap om Hallands floder. 
Nilsen upptäckte dessutom att så fort lärarna uppmanade barnen att reflektera över vad de gjorde i det pedagogiska spelet tröttnade de och gick därifrån.”

Så många frågor om detta. För det första, hur kan Hallands floder fortfarande vara ett case för viktig ”bestående kunskap”. För det andra, om samlandet av ”poäng” gör att man inte tillägnar sig kunskap... har ni hört talas om prov? Hur många gånger har man inte bankat in något bara för att poäng och glömma det dagen därpå?
Och slutligen: ”så fort lärarna uppmanade barnen att reflektera gick de där ifrån”. Du menar ”så fort lärarna tog över och bad barnen sluta spela spelet för att lyssna på dem så gick de där ifrån”. Det kanske säger mer om lärarna än spelet 😂

## 137. 2019-04-20 🔴 (8487 chars)

**call:** `[ ] voice`  `[ ] thinking`  `[ ] skip`  `[ ] private`

```
Three generations is all it takes to change.

Edit: Behind paywall. I'm posting the full text here, just to exemplify what kind of post will be filtered according to the new EU copyright law...

"Every friday lunchtime, Washington’s Church of the Epiphany near the White House turns into a mosque. Hundreds of Muslims prostrate themselves in the direction of Mecca on carpets spread on the ground (pictured). The congregation includes Homeland Security and fbi agents, State Department bureaucrats and a posse of lawyers from the Department of Justice. The imam is a Treasury official. His sermons steer clear of politics.

America’s Muslims have come a long way since some of their ancestors arrived as slaves from West Africa in the 16th century. From the late 19th century to the 1920s a wave of well-off Arabs came to study and stayed on, entering the ranks of America’s middle class. In a nation of immigrants, Muslims found it easier to fit in than in Europe with its more settled population. Except in a few cities such as Dearborn, Michigan, Muslims in America are thinly spread, totalling about 3.5m, or 1.1% of the population.

Europe’s relationship with Islam has been longer, deeper and more conflicted. The religion had previously entered Europe in the eighth century in Spain under a caliphate and again in the early 14th century in south-eastern Europe under the Ottomans. Both times it came in by the sword and was driven out more than half a millennium later. In the 20th century the Muslims in Europe were different from America’s, too. Millions remained after the Ottoman armies were defeated, and new ones were brought in as soldiers and workers. European powers drafted some 3.5m Muslims from their colonies to fight two world wars. Most went home afterwards, but more arrived to repair the war damage.

In the two decades after 1945 western European governments recruited hundreds of thousands of migrant labourers from far-flung places. Britain brought in Pakistanis from the Kashmiri mountains and the highlands of Bangladesh’s Sylhet; France turned to its north African territories; and Germany imported workers from Turkey’s Anatolian hills. They were expected to leave when their work was done, but instead fetched their families. Germany took its time to grant them and their German-born children citizenship. More recently an outpouring of asylum-seekers from the Muslim world’s many conflicts has changed the demography. Between 2014 and 2016 alone about 1m migrants arrived in Europe, most of them Arab. Germany took in half of them.

They asked for workers, and people came
Leaving out Russia and Turkey, Europe is now home to about 26m Muslims, who account for about 5% of its population and are typically much younger than the locals. In many European cities Muhammad (in its various spellings) has become the most popular name for a child.

Precise numbers are hard to pin down. Besides, Muslims are not a homogeneous group; they differ by religious practice, culture and ethnicity. Their experience also varies from country to country. British law protects diversity in religion and practice, whereas in France the display of religious symbols, including the veil, is banned in most public institutions, including schools. Yet French Muslims tend to be less religious than British ones, and non-Muslims in France are happier to have Muslims as neighbours and more likely to marry one.

In some ways the 20th-century wave of Muslim arrivals in the West has done remarkably well. Many of them went from the mostly illiterate edges of the Islamic world to industrial cities. They often came from large families. Their children have gone a long way to closing the gaps in education, salary and lifestyles with their adopted countries.

A third generation of Muslim millennials feels more confident both of its Western identity and its Islam
Muslims are also becoming increasingly prominent in Western politics. In November’s midterm elections, Americans voted two Muslim women, Rashida Tlaib and Ilhan Omar, into Congress for the first time. London, Europe’s largest city, has a Muslim mayor, Sadiq Khan. The continent’s largest port, Rotterdam, has a Moroccan-born one, Ahmed Aboutaleb. And Muslims play a large part in Western entertainment, sports and fashion.

But the past two decades have been marred by violence and fear, too. Since 2000 more than 3,670 people have been killed in jihadist attacks in the West, 2,996 of them in America on September 11th 2001 alone. Over the same period 119 people died in anti-Muslim assaults. Jihadists make up a minuscule fringe of Muslims in the West, but those terrorist attacks turned Islam into a looming threat in many Western minds. Far-right parties fed on, and fanned, such fears. Even short of violence, the relationship between Muslims and their Western host countries was often wary or worse.

America’s Muslims until fairly recently considered themselves a cut above Europe’s. They were more middle-class, more integrated and enjoyed a more harmonious relationship with their chosen country. But a combination of America’s involvement in the Middle East, the jihadist reaction to it and a concurrent surge of white nationalism has disturbed the harmony. In a survey in 2017, 42% of Muslim schoolchildren in America said they were bullied because of their faith. One in five Americans would deny Muslim citizens the right to vote. President Donald Trump encouraged such hostility during his election campaign, pledging a “total and complete shutdown of Muslims entering the United States”. Soon after coming to office he tried to impose a visa ban on six mainly Muslim countries. And last month he stirred fears of Muslim immigration again by suggesting that prayer mats had been left at the Mexican border where he wants to build a wall.

This report will explore how Muslim identity has been moulded by external and internal pressures since the mass migration to the West began in the 1950s. It will trace the impact of the laissez-faire approach Western governments initially adopted to the incoming faith and then of increasingly interventionist policies as the Muslim population grew and the relationship became more troubled. It will explore how Muslim communities have responded to policies designed to aid assimilation or improve security.

The report will also look at the generational shifts within Muslim communities as their members have adapted to life in the West. Flexibility and pluralism helped Islam flourish as a global religion for 1,400 years, but recently in the West Muslims have had to devise a theology for living as a small minority among non-Muslims, not as rulers. This is still a work in progress. The first generation of Muslim immigrants largely accepted the West as they found it and kept a low profile, unsure how long they would be staying. They brought their rituals and traditions with them and looked to their countries of origin to cater for their spiritual needs. Imams came from Turkey, north Africa and South Asia. Some Muslim countries funded the building and running of mosques.

As ties with the West became stronger, those with the incomers’ countries of origin diminished. Religion became more important than ethnicity as a marker of identity. The second generation of Muslims in the West rejected the quiet and submissive faith of their parents and looked for preachers who spoke their language and understood their concerns, often online. They wanted a religion that empowered them. At the extreme end, a few embraced violence. Jihadists are overwhelmingly either second-generation Muslims or converts.

A third generation of Muslim millennials feels more confident both of its Western identity and its Islam. It has the tools to negotiate politics and the justice system, and to interact with the establishment. Religion is increasingly becoming a matter of individual choice. The 10,000-plus mosques in the West represent the entire spectrum of Islamic belief and practice, from the Deobandis (see glossary) to women-led prayer. Many have left the faith altogether.

Past and recent experience has made Muslims wary of taking their future in the West for granted. But if the mainstream prevails, they are about to embark on a new phase. Three generations after their arrival, they are fashioning a theology for highly diverse societies and secular systems of government in which Islam does not hold power. In short, they are building a Western Islam."
```

## 145. 2019-07-19 🔴 (2101 chars)

**call:** `[ ] voice`  `[ ] thinking`  `[ ] skip`  `[ ] private`

```
Stockholms bultande hjärta väcks till liv varje sommar. Genom tusentals ideella timmar skapas öppna mötesplatser där alla är välkomna att uttrycka sig, dela med sig, skratta, dansa och drömma under den Svenska natthimlen. Denna kulturrörelse är bland det finaste vi har i stan och en av anledningarna jag blev kär i vår huvudstad när jag flyttade hit. I en kall stad där blickar viks bort på gatan och var man har ett eget säte i tunnelbanan, så var det befriande att hitta platser där främlingar faktiskt ser varandra i ögonen! Utan att döma, utan att kräva, utan bara för att dela glädje och lugn i att se och bli sedd!

Men, glada, dansande människor är ju såklart ett hot mot ordningen och bör prioriteras över gängkrig och våldtäktsutredningar. ”Ring 112”, föreslår konstapeln, för en elektronisk musikslinga som kan höras över fjärden är tydligen i paritet med pågående inbrott eller hjärtstillestånd.
Oförståndet och ointresset från politiker och tjänstemän att förstå varför tusentals människor söker sig till dessa platser. Fördomarna och de rena lögner som sprids av både polis och lättkränkta ”vänner av ordning”, utbasunerat utan ifrågasättande av media.
Stockholm skall vara tyst, kallt och stängt.

Var som ofta glöms bort är hur tätt sammankopplat den fria kulturen är innovation och kreativitet. Festivalen Burning Man ligger inte några timmar från San Francisco av en slump. Det är en systerstad till Silicon Valley, sprungen ur samma jord, med ett delat DNA. Att tro att Stockholm skall hålla sig i framkant av innovation, design och kreativitet internationellt och samtidigt tro att vi skall städa upp varenda bakgata och släcka varenda kulturyttring som inte passar våra mellanmjölkskartonger är naivt och rent okunnigt.

Låt människor få leva! Vi har inte många månader på oss att faktiskt göra det i denna kalla mörka stad. Låt oss leva, så lovar vi att vi skall gå tillbaka i våra hålor och bygga nya Spotify, Paradox eller Tocaboca när vintermörker faller på.

Låt oss få dansa i sommarnatten, eller ännu bättre, kom och dansa med oss! Det finns kramar så det räcker till alla!
```

Att ungdomar i Danderyd knarkar mer är väl lika självklart som att som nån från SEB är med på en Stureplansfest så finns det kokain? Tycker det är fantastiskt att Löfvén pekar ut det uppenbara - knark måste man betala för!

Kristersson kontrar med att "Det är varken mindre eller mer ungdomar i Djursholm missbrukar narkotika" vilket inte är sant (Google it). Sedan fortsätter med floskler som att polisen skall lägga mer fokus på knark och vi skall ha nya lagar för att övervaka folk (avskaffa posthemligheten).

De som velat knarka har fortsatt göra det, och samtidigt byggt upp en trygg finansieringskälla for global organiserad brottslighet.

## 152. 2019-09-02 🔴 (1733 chars)

**call:** `[ ] voice`  `[ ] thinking`  `[ ] skip`  `[ ] private`

```
Sverige har problem: vi lånar för lite. Stadsskulden måste öka för att skapa en både långsiktigt och kortsiktigt tryggare finansiell grund.

Låter det baklänges?

Konstigt nog finns det två viktiga anledningar till att inte låna för lite som land. Den första är såklart att räntorna internationellt är så låga att vi ganska lätt skulle kunna göra investeringar som har bättre avkastning än räntekostnaderna.
Men det finns en annan aspekt som är lite mer komplex: Om man inte lånar blir det svårare att låna när man vill låna. För att marknaden för svenska stadsobligationer skall vara "likvid" (dvs. att man kan köpa eller sälja snabbt, i volym, utan att påverka priset), så krävs det att den har en viss volym. På en stor marknad är det lätt att matcha köpare och säljare, men på en liten så blir risken större att du kanske inte hittar nån som vill köpa för det verkliga värdet, vilket tvingar dig att dumpa ditt pris för att få sålt.
Allt eftersom marknaden på Svenska stadsobligationer glesas ut, så minskas Sveriges möjlighet att ge ut större mängder obligationer, eftersom det skulle leda till en prisdumpning. Alltså, paradoxalt nog: På grund av att vi lånat för lite så kommer det bli svårare att låna mer när krisen kommer.

Låter det fortfarande baklänges?

Jag kan rekommendera kursen "Economics of Money and Banking" på Columbia University, som jag nyligen tagit på Coursera. Läste dagens DN och insåg att hade jag inte tagit denna kursen hade allt låtit lite mer baklänges:
https://www.coursera.org/learn/money-banking

Ps. Om nån väljer att gå kursen, så träffas jag gärna upp för en fika och diskuterar innehållet. Jag har varit mind blown så många gånger de senaste månaderna att jag behöver nån att prata av mig med.
```

Some guts right there...

"This is all wrong. I shouldn’t be standing here. I should be back in school on the other side of the ocean. Yet you all come to me for hope? How dare you! You have stolen my dreams and my childhood with your empty words. And yet I’m one of the lucky ones. People are suffering. People are dying. Entire ecosystems are collapsing. We are in the beginning of a mass extinction. And all you can talk about is money and fairytales of eternal economic growth. How dare you!

For more than 30 years the science has been crystal clear. How dare you continue to look away, and come here saying that you are doing enough, when the politics and solutions needed are still nowhere in sight.

You say you “hear” us and that you understand the urgency. But no matter how sad and angry I am, I don’t want to believe that. Because if you fully understood the situation and still kept on failing to act, then you would be evil. And I refuse to believe that.

The popular idea of cutting our emissions in half in 10 years only gives us a 50% chance of staying below 1.5C degrees, and the risk of setting off irreversible chain reactions beyond human control.

Maybe 50% is acceptable to you. But those numbers don’t include tipping points, most feedback loops, additional warming hidden by toxic air pollution or the aspects of justice and equity. They also rely on my and my children’s generation sucking hundreds of billions of tonnes of your CO2 out of the air with technologies that barely exist. So a 50% risk is simply not acceptable to us – we who have to live with the consequences.

To have a 67% chance of staying below a 1.5C global temperature rise – the best odds given by the Intergovernmental Panel on Climate Change – the world had 420 gigatonnes of carbon dioxide left to emit back on 1 January 2018. Today that figure is already down to less than 350 gigatonnes. How dare you pretend that this can be solved with business-as-usual and some technical solutions. With today’s emissions levels, that remaining CO2 budget will be entirely gone in less than eight and a half years.

There will not be any solutions or plans presented in line with these figures today. Because these numbers are too uncomfortable. And you are still not mature enough to tell it like it is.

You are failing us. But the young people are starting to understand your betrayal. The eyes of all future generations are upon you. And if you choose to fail us I say we will never forgive you. We will not let you get away with this. Right here, right now is where we draw the line. The world is waking up. And change is coming, whether you like it or not."
```
